26struct Glyph {
27 double left;
28 double right;
29 std::vector<std::vector<std::pair<double, double>>> strokes;
30
31 Glyph() : left(0.0), right(0.0) {}
38 Glyph(double l, double r, std::vector<std::vector<std::pair<double, double>>> s)
39 : left(l), right(r), strokes(std::move(s)) {}
40};
41
45class Roboto {
46public:
48 static Roboto &instance() {
49 static Roboto inst;
50 return inst;
51 }
52
63 std::string render(const std::string &text, double x, double y, double size, const std::string &anchor = "start") {
64 double scale = size; // Glyphs are normalized to EM square of size 1.0
65 std::vector<uint32_t> codes = utf8ToUnicode(text);
66
67 double total_width = 0.0;
68 for (uint32_t c : codes) {
69 if (glyphs_.count(c)) {
70 total_width += (glyphs_[c].right - glyphs_[c].left) * scale;
71 }
72 }
73
74 double cur_x = x;
75 if (anchor == "middle")
76 cur_x -= total_width / 2.0;
77 else if (anchor == "end")
78 cur_x -= total_width;
79
80 std::string path_data;
81 for (uint32_t c : codes) {
82 if (glyphs_.count(c)) {
83 const auto &g = glyphs_[c];
84 double offset_x = cur_x; // since left is 0.0, offset_x is just cur_x
85 for (const auto &stroke : g.strokes) {
86 for (size_t i = 0; i < stroke.size(); ++i) {
87 double px = offset_x + stroke[i].first * scale;
88 double py = y - stroke[i].second * scale; // Flip Y direction (TTF Y is up, SVG Y is down)
89 if (i == 0)
90 path_data += std::format("M {:.2f} {:.2f} ", px, py);
91 else
92 path_data += std::format("L {:.2f} {:.2f} ", px, py);
93 }
94 if (!stroke.empty()) {
95 path_data += "Z ";
96 }
97 }
98 cur_x += g.right * scale; // Advance by the width
99 }
100 }
101
102 return path_data;
103 }
104
105private:
106 std::map<uint32_t, Glyph> glyphs_;
107
108 Roboto() {
109 auto add = [&](uint32_t c, double l, double r, const std::vector<std::vector<std::pair<double, double>>> &s) {
110 glyphs_[c] = Glyph(l, r, s);
111 };

237
243 std::vector<uint32_t> utf8ToUnicode(const std::string &str) {
244 std::vector<uint32_t> unicode;
245 for (size_t i = 0; i < str.length();) {
246 unsigned char c = str[i];
247 if (c < 0x80) {
248 unicode.push_back(c);
249 i++;
250 } else if ((c & 0xE0) == 0xC0) {
251 if (i + 1 < str.length()) {
252 unicode.push_back(((c & 0x1F) << 6) | (str[i + 1] & 0x3F));
253 i += 2;
254 } else {
255 i++;
256 }
257 } else if ((c & 0xF0) == 0xE0) {
258 if (i + 2 < str.length()) {
259 uint32_t val = ((c & 0x0F) << 12) | ((str[i + 1] & 0x3F) << 6) | (str[i + 2] & 0x3F);
260 unicode.push_back(val);
261 i += 3;
262 } else {
263 i++;
264 }
265 } else {
266 i++;
267 }
268 }
269 return unicode;
270 }
271};
